function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 15') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.15!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// Dir added: dev
@mkdir('dev');
if (!is_dir('dev')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: dev');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of dev');
}

// File added: dev/.htaccess
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('dev/.htaccess', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('T3JkZXIgRGVueSxBbGxvdwpEZW55IEZyb20gQWxsCgo='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('dev/.htaccess') && (sha1_file('dev/.htaccess') != '2e61197b1437bb55c9d20379ff16969a9f872967')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/.htaccess');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/.htaccess');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/.htaccess')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/.htaccess', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/.htaccess')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/.htaccess');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/.htaccess') != '2e61197b1437bb55c9d20379ff16969a9f872967') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/.htaccess');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/.htaccess', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/.htaccess');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'ecd9036a5ffe7f8c52fc983b7e5e8dcc4b5e2f82') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ecd9036a5ffe7f8c52fc983b7e5e8dcc4b5e2f82') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '26192b05fc5ff71302d8f022d590113d615964d4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ecd9036a5ffe7f8c52fc983b7e5e8dcc4b5e2f82') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql') != 'c55182b04c3ec8b971522d72191eb0f58cc6c65a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql') !== 'c55182b04c3ec8b971522d72191eb0f58cc6c65a') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql') !== '51df9ff02dc2217a6d523c261b5044182bb34b3b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql') !== 'c55182b04c3ec8b971522d72191eb0f58cc6c65a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_ids.sql');
		}
	}
}

	if (!is_file('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') != 'b98b386a7ad7f596c8ef64af44f6efedd917eec0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== 'b98b386a7ad7f596c8ef64af44f6efedd917eec0') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-ietf-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== 'b98b386a7ad7f596c8ef64af44f6efedd917eec0') {
